    <script>
     function sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline () {
    if (sr_detect_operaMini || !("classList" in document.createElement("_"))) {
	return false;
    }
    var nav_trigger = document.getElementById('nav_trigger');
    if(!nav_trigger || nav_trigger.triggered) {
	return false;
    }
    nav_trigger.triggered = true;
    var nav = document.getElementById('nav');
    var nav_trigger_a = nav_trigger.querySelector('a');
    if (nav_trigger_a) {
	nav_trigger_a.setAttribute('href','javascript:void(0)');
	nav_trigger.onclick = function (event) {
	    nav.classList.toggle('open');
	    var is_open = nav.classList.contains('open');
	    if (is_open) {
		nav_trigger.classList.add('open');
	    }
	    else {
		nav_trigger.classList.remove('open');
	    }
	    event.preventDefault();
	    try { sr_record_analytics_event('MainNavButtonClick_inline',sr_record_directory(),sr_record_page());}
	    catch(err) {}
	};
    }
    return true;
}
sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline();
    </script>

      <h2>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/?ref=br&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Stathead
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="adblock">
       <p>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/?ref=br&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball" target="_blank">
         <img alt="Stathead.com Logo" onerror="this.src='https://d2p3bygnnzw9w3.cloudfront.net/req/202004233/logos/stathead-logo.png'; this.onerror = null;" src="https://d2p3bygnnzw9w3.cloudfront.net/req/202004233/logos/stathead-br.svg" style="max-width:70%"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <div>
        <h4>
         The Most Powerful Research Tools in Sports.
        </h4>
        <p>
         Find any player, any team, any season, any game, any play.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p>
        <a class="button stathead_button" href="https://stathead.com/?ref=br&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball" target="_blank">
         <strong>
          Subscribe Now
         </strong>
         (First Month Free)
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Season and Career Finder
       </h4>
       Find single-season or multi-year totals to create leaderboards by team, position, age, and more.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/loHpo?&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
         Which pitching staff threw the most pitches in a season (since 1988)?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/season_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/season_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Pitching
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/team-season-finder.cgi?type=b&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/team-season-finder.cgi?type=p&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Pitching
       </a>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Game Finder
       </h4>
       Find individual games matching a variety of criteria. Includes options for postseason games and All-Star Games.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/tELfN?&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
         Who hit four home runs in a single game?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/game_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/game_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Pitching
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/game_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;class=team&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/game_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;class=team&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Pitching
       </a>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Split Finder
       </h4>
       Find leaders matching a various split criteria. Can also be used to compare values in the split to the player's overall total.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/k2gLb?&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
         Which pitcher allowed the most home runs to fellow pitchers?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/split_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/split_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Pitching
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/split_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;class=team&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/split_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;class=team&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Pitching
       </a>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Streak Finder
       </h4>
       Find streaks of games for teams or players. Includes options postseason and All-Star games.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/NUBH0?&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
         Who reached base in the most consecutive playoff games?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/streak_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/streak_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Player Pitching
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/streak_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;class=team&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Batting
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/streak_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;class=team&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Team Pitching
       </a>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Event Finder
       </h4>
       Find individual plays matching a variety of criteria and get a summary line for all matching plays
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/XQdqD?&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
         Which pitcher recorded the most bases loaded strikeouts in 2019?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/event_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Batting by Team
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/event_finder.cgi?type=p&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
        Pitching by Team
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/baseball/event_finder.cgi?type=b&amp;as=1&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=br_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=baseball">
